# 青娥丸及不同拆方组合水提物对正常小鼠急性毒性影响的实验研究

## 1. 文献基础信息

- **title**: 青娥丸及不同拆方组合水提物对正常小鼠急性毒性影响的实验研究 (Experimental Study on Acute Toxicity of Qing 'e Pills and Their Separated Prescriptions Aqueous Extract in Normal Mice)
- **authors**: 郭欣 (Guo Xin), 蔡涛涛 (Cai Taotao), 黄娜娜 (HUANG Nana), 孙蓉 (Sun Rong)
- **journal**: 中国药物警戒 (Chinese Journal of Pharmacovigilance)
- **year**: 2021
- **doi_or_pmid**: 10.19803/j.1672-8629.2021.05.06
- **full_text_link**: Not specified in the article
- **is_open_access**: Not specified in the article

## 2. 化合物信息

- **compound_name**: 青娥丸及不同拆方组合水提物 (Qing'e Pills and their separated prescriptions aqueous extract). The study evaluated five different combinations:
- **Combination 1**: 盐杜仲 (salt Eucommia ulmoides) + 盐补骨脂 (salt Psoralea corylifolia) + 炒核桃仁 (fried Juglans regia)
- **Combination 2**: 盐杜仲 (salt Eucommia ulmoides) + 盐补骨脂 (salt Psoralea corylifolia)
- **Combination 3**: 盐补骨脂 (salt Psoralea corylifolia) + 大蒜 (Allium sativum)
- **Combination 4**: 盐补骨脂 (salt Psoralea corylifolia) + 炒核桃仁 (fried Juglans regia) + 大蒜 (Allium sativum)
- **Combination 5**: 青娥丸全方 (Qing'e pills complete formula)
- **synonyms**: Not applicable
- **cas_number**: Not applicable
- **molecular_formula**: Not applicable
- **molecular_weight**: Not applicable
- **smiles**: Not applicable
- **inchi_key**: Not applicable
- **source**: Individual herbs were purchased from Shandong Baitang Chinese Medicine Yinpian Co., Ltd. and the local market; aqueous extracts were prepared in the laboratory.
- **purity**: The content of two marker compounds, psoralen and isopsoralen, was determined in the aqueous extracts:
- **Psoralen**: 0.1563% (Combo 1), 0.1726% (Combo 2), 0.1048% (Combo 3), 0.0503% (Combo 4), 0.0838% (Combo 5)
- **Isopsoralen**: 0.1606% (Combo 1), 0.1589% (Combo 2), 0.0960% (Combo 3), 0.0366% (Combo 4), 0.0623% (Combo 5)
- **category_usage**: Traditional Chinese Medicine, used for nourishing the kidney and strengthening the waist.
- **structure_image**: Not specified in the article

## 3. 实验设计

### 3.1 动物模型

- **species**: Mus musculus (Mice)
- **strain**: Kunming
- **sex**: Male and female, half each
- **age**: Not specified in the article (described as "适龄" - appropriate age)
- **weight**: 18-22 g
- **housing_conditions**: SPF grade

### 3.2 分组与给药

- **group_info**: 6 groups: Normal Control group, and 5 treatment groups (Combination 1-5). n=20 per group for the formal experiment.
- **doses**: This was a Maximum Tolerated Dose (MTD) study. Doses are reported as g of crude drug per kg body weight per day [g/(kg·d)]:
- **Combination 1**: 165.32
- **Combination 2**: 156.52
- **Combination 3**: 156.00
- **Combination 4**: 118.78
- **Combination 5**: 129.84
- **administration_route**: Gavage
- **dosing_frequency**: Once
- **treatment_duration**: Single administration within one day.
- **observation_period**: 14 days
- **license_or_permit**: SYXK (鲁) 20140001

## 4. 毒性结果

- **ld50**: LD₅₀ could not be determined, so a Maximum Tolerated Dose (MTD) study was performed.
- **noael_loael**: Not specified in the article
- **mortality**:
- **Each Combination Group (1-5)**: 1/20 died in each group.
- **clinical_signs**:
- **activity_changes**: Depression (精神不佳), inactivity (怠动), ataxia (共济失调), stiffness (僵住), proneness (俯卧), clonic convulsion (阵挛性惊厥).
- **appetite_weight**: Not specified in the article.
- **fur_behavior**: Different degrees of redness and swelling in ears, tails, and eyes were observed in all groups. Group 2 also showed hair loss. Group 5 (full formula) showed no obvious abnormalities.
- **body_weight_changes**: Weight gain in treated groups was slower than in the control group, but the difference was not statistically significant.
- **toxicity_classification**: Not specified in the article.

## 5. 器官毒性与病理学

### 5.1 器官检查

- **gross_pathology**:
- **liver**: No obvious abnormalities observed on necropsy of the deceased mice.
- **kidney**: No obvious abnormalities observed on necropsy of the deceased mice.
- **heart**: No obvious abnormalities observed on necropsy of the deceased mice.
- **spleen**: No obvious abnormalities observed on necropsy of the deceased mice.
- **lung**: No obvious abnormalities observed on necropsy of the deceased mice.
- **others**: No obvious abnormalities observed in the brain, stomach, or small intestine on necropsy.
- **organ_weight_ratios**: Not specified in the article
- **gross_observation**: No obvious abnormalities were seen in the major organs upon necropsy of the single deceased mouse in each group.
![Mice in each group on the seventh day after administration](./images/Qing_e_Pill_mice_day7.png)

### 5.2 组织病理（HE染色）

- **histopathology**:
- **liver**: Liver lobule structure was clear, with radial arrangement of hepatic cords. Hepatocytes were polygonal with central nuclei. No degeneration, necrosis, or inflammatory cell infiltration was observed.
- **kidney**: The cortex and medulla were clearly demarcated. The glomeruli were mainly composed of capillaries, and the Bowman's space was clearly visible. There was no degeneration or necrosis of renal tubules, and no interstitial inflammatory cell infiltration or fibrosis.
- **heart**: Not examined.
- **spleen**: Not examined.
- **lung**: Not examined.
- **others**: Not examined.
- **pathology_scoring**: Not specified in the article
- **histology_images**:
- **liver**: ./images/Qing_e_Pill_liver_HE.png
 ![Liver pathology of mice in each group](./images/Qing_e_Pill_liver_HE.png)
- **kidney**: ./images/Qing_e_Pill_kidney_HE.png
 ![Kidney pathology of mice in each group](./images/Qing_e_Pill_kidney_HE.png)
- **heart**: Not specified in the article
- **spleen**: Not specified in the article
- **lung**: Not specified in the article
- **others**: Not specified in the article

## 6. 血液生化与生理指标

- **alt_ast**: All drug groups showed elevated ALT and AST levels. For ALT, groups 1, 2, 3 showed a highly significant difference (P<0.001) from the control.
- **akp**: All drug groups showed elevated ALP levels, with groups 1, 4 showing a highly significant difference (P<0.001).
- **bun_cr**: BUN and Cr levels were elevated in groups 2, 3, and 4, showing a significant difference from the control group (P<0.01).
- **hematology**: Not specified in the article
- **cytokines**: Not specified in the article
- **other_parameters**: Not specified in the article

| 组别 (Group) | ALT (IU/L) | AST (IU/L) | ALP (金氏单位/100mL) | BUN (mmol/L) | Cr (μmol/L) |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| **正常组 (Normal)** | 59.02±28.88 | 145.53±63.29 | 63.97±10.09 | 7.62±1.09 | 87.23±16.27 |
| **组合1 (Combo 1)** | 122.37±40.07\*\*\* | 209.67±75.96 | 89.55±7.90\*\*\* | 10.49±1.54\*\* | 145.32±16.41\*\* |
| **组合2 (Combo 2)** | 139.16±29.03\*\*\* | 231.36±117.03 | 80.92±20.59\* | 9.86±1.05\*\*\* | 151.09±40.83\*\* |
| **组合3 (Combo 3)** | 146.54±42.65\*\*\* | 303.82±125.80\*\* | 81.23±18.69\* | 9.09±0.71\*\* | 90.62±12.42\* |
| **组合4 (Combo 4)** | 132.56±73.92\*\* | 281.50±148.72\* | 87.09±11.90\*\*\* | 8.65±1.54\* | 122.05±8.90 |
| **组合5 (Combo 5)** | 108.33±57.41\* | 222.99±196.57 | 70.91±11.13\* | 11.57±0.80\* | 97.58±9.54 |

_注: 与正常对照组比较, \*P<0.05, \*\*P<0.01, \*\*\*P<0.001 _

## 7. 曲线拟合与效力参数

- **dose_response_model**: Not applicable
- **ec50_ac50**: Not applicable
- **emax**: Not applicable

## 8. 作者结论与备注

- **作者主要结论**: The acute toxicity of all tested combinations is lower than that of salt Psoralea corylifolia alone (reported previously by the lab as LD₅₀ of 56.028 g/kg). This suggests that the compatibility of herbs in the Qing'e Pill formula according to traditional Chinese medicine principles can reduce the acute toxicity of Psoralea corylifolia. The full formula (Combination 5) showed the highest relative safety.
- **潜在毒性机制（如有）**: The authors speculate that Psoralen and Isopsoralen from Psoralea corylifolia are the toxic basis. However, the measured content of these compounds did not directly correlate with the observed order of toxicity among the groups, suggesting the mechanism is more complex and requires further study. The combination is thought to reduce toxicity through the principles of traditional Chinese medicine, where the properties of other herbs moderate the harshness of Psoralea corylifolia.
- **是否支持构建预测模型**: Yes, this study provides MTD values for several complex herbal mixtures and links them to the content of known toxic components, making it valuable data for modeling the toxicity of traditional medicine formulas.
- **研究局限性**: The toxic material basis was not definitively identified, as the content of psoralen/isopsoralen did not correlate with toxicity. The study also presents a contradiction where blood biochemistry indicates liver/kidney damage, but histopathology shows no changes.
- **你的备注或判断**: The study effectively demonstrates the principle of "compatibility and toxicity reduction" in traditional Chinese medicine using a standard acute toxicity limit test. A notable finding is the significant discrepancy between blood biochemistry markers, which clearly indicated organ stress (hepatotoxicity and nephrotoxicity), and the histopathology results, which were reported as normal. This suggests that the damage might have been functional or at a level not detectable by standard H&E staining, warranting further investigation.

---
# 青楷槭对小鼠急性毒性及体外抗弓形虫作用研究

## 1. 文献基础信息

- authors: 尹雄杰, 孙明月, 徐燕, 金春梅, 金丽丽, 张长浩
- journal: Journal of Medical Science Yanbian University
- year: 2020
- doi_or_pmid: 10.16068/j.1000-1824.2020.04.002
- full_text_link: http://www.cnki.net
- is_open_access: 否

## 2. 化合物信息  

- compound_name: 青楷槭 (Acer tegmentosum)

# Experimental Comparison Study on Mice's Acute Toxicity of Different Composition in Cortex Periplocae

## 1. 文献基础信息

- **title**: 香加皮不同组分对小鼠急性毒性实验比较研究 (Experimental Comparison Study on Mice's Acute Toxicity of Different Composition in Cortex Periplocae)
- **authors**: SUN Rong, BAO Zhi-ye, HUANG Wei, LV Li-li, ZHANG Zuo-ping, REN Hai-yong
- **journal**: 中国药物警戒 (Chinese Journal of Pharmacovigilance)
- **year**: 2010
- **doi_or_pmid**: Article ID: 1672-8629 (2010) 10-0579-06
- **full_text_link**: Not specified in the article
- **is_open_access**: Not specified in the article

## 2. 化合物信息

- **compound_name**: 香加皮 (Cortex Periplocae), from the plant *Periploca sepium Bge.*. The study tested three different preparations:
- **All-components**: Crude drug preparation.
- **Water extract**: Aqueous extract of the crude drug.
- **Alcohol extract**: 60% ethanol extract of the crude drug.
- **synonyms**: Not applicable
- **cas_number**: Not specified in the article
- **molecular_formula**: Not applicable
- **molecular_weight**: Not applicable
- **smiles**: Not applicable
- **inchi_key**: Not applicable
- **source**: The extracts were prepared in the laboratory from the crude drug.
- **purity**: Not specified in the article
- **category_usage**: Traditional Chinese Medicine
- **structure_image**: Not specified in the article

## 3. 实验设计

### 3.1 动物模型

- **species**: Mus musculus (Mice)
- **strain**: Not specified in the article
- **sex**: Not specified in the article
- **age**: Not specified in the article
- **weight**: 18-22 g
- **housing_conditions**: Not specified in the article

### 3.2 分组与给药

- **group_info**:
- **All-components**: 1 treatment group and 1 control group, n=20 per group.
- **Water extract**: 5 treatment groups and 1 control group, n=20 per group.
- **Alcohol extract**: 5 treatment groups and 1 control group, n=20 per group.
- **doses**:
- **All-components (MTD test)**: 16.0 g/kg·d
- **Water extract (LD₅₀ test)**: 115.0, 102.4, 91.1, 81.1, 72.2 g/kg
- **Alcohol extract (LD₅₀ test)**: 85.75, 73.00, 62.00, 52.75, 44.75 g/kg
- **administration_route**: Oral gavage (implied from methodology)
- **dosing_frequency**: Single administration
- **treatment_duration**: Single dose
- **observation_period**: 14 days
- **license_or_permit**: SCXK(鲁)20090001

## 4. 毒性结果

- **ld50**:
- **All-components**: LD₅₀ could not be determined; MTD was 16.0 g/kg·d.
- **Water extract**: LD₅₀ = 93.578 g/kg·d (95% CI: 89.149 - 98.484 g/kg·d).
- **Alcohol extract**: LD₅₀ = 61.388 g/kg·d (95% CI: 57.466 - 65.521 g/kg·d).
- **noael_loael**: Not specified in the article
- **mortality**:
- **Water Extract**:

| Dose (g/kg) | Number of Animals | Deaths | Mortality Rate (%) |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 115.0 | 20 | 18 | 90 |
| 102.4 | 20 | 13 | 65 |
| 91.1 | 20 | 10 | 50 |
| 81.1 | 20 | 5 | 25 |
| 72.2 | 20 | 0 | 0 |

- **Alcohol Extract**:

| Dose (g/kg) | Number of Animals | Deaths | Mortality Rate (%) |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 85.75 | 20 | 20 | 100 |
| 73.00 | 20 | 14 | 70 |
| 62.00 | 20 | 10 | 50 |
| 52.75 | 20 | 6 | 30 |
| 44.75 | 20 | 1 | 5 |

- **clinical_signs**:
- **activity_changes**: The main toxic symptoms included convulsions, tetraplegia, and respiratory depression.
- **appetite_weight**: Not specified in the article.
- **fur_behavior**: Diarrhoea was observed as a main toxic symptom. Deaths primarily occurred within 48 hours for both water and alcohol extract groups.
- **body_weight_changes**: Mice in the treatment groups for both water and alcohol extracts showed a significant decrease in body weight during the first few days post-administration compared to the control group, followed by a gradual recovery in the surviving animals.
- **toxicity_classification**: Not specified in the article

## 5. 器官毒性与病理学

### 5.1 器官检查

- **gross_pathology**: Not specified in the article
- **organ_weight_ratios**: Not specified in the article
- **gross_observation**: Not specified in the article

### 5.2 组织病理（HE染色）

- **histopathology**: Not specified in the article
- **pathology_scoring**: Not specified in the article
- **histology_images**: Not specified in the article

## 6. 血液生化与生理指标

- **alt_ast**: Not specified in the article
- **akp**: Not specified in the article
- **tbil**: Not specified in the article
- **bun_cr**: Not specified in the article
- **hematology**: Not specified in the article
- **cytokines**: Not specified in the article
- **other_parameters**: Not specified in the article

## 7. 曲线拟合与效力参数

- **dose_response_model**: LD₅₀ was calculated using the Bliss method.
- **ec50_ac50**: Not applicable
- **emax**: Not applicable

## 8. 作者结论与备注

- **作者主要结论**: The acute toxicity of the different Cortex Periplocae components in mice follows the order: alcohol extract > water extract > all-components.
- **潜在毒性机制（如有）**: Not specified in the article. The toxic symptoms, including convulsions and respiratory depression, suggest a potential impact on the central nervous system.
- **是否支持构建预测模型**: Yes, the study provides quantitative LD₅₀ values with confidence intervals for two different extracts and an MTD for a third, which is valuable data for modeling the toxicity of herbal preparations based on their extraction method.
- **研究局限性**: The study lacks pathological (gross and histopathology) and biochemical analysis, which would provide a more complete picture of organ-specific toxicity. The specific chemical constituents responsible for the toxicity were not identified.
- **你的备注或判断**: The study provides a clear comparison of the acute toxicity of three different preparations of Cortex Periplocae using standard LD₅₀ and MTD methodologies. The finding that the alcohol extract is most toxic and the crude (all-components) preparation is least toxic is significant for clinical safety considerations. The data is robust for an acute lethality study, but the absence of pathology and bloodwork limits the understanding of the underlying toxic mechanisms.

---

# 食品包装材料PE热收缩膜的小鼠急性毒性试验

## 1. 文献基础信息  

- title: 食品包装材料PE热收缩膜的小鼠急性毒性试验 / Acute Toxicity Test of Polyethylene Heat-shrinkable Membranes in Food Packaging Materials
- authors: 庄思琪, 敬明武, 葛宇杰, 蒋中仁, 徐薇
- journal: 职业卫生与病伤 (Occupational Health and Damage)
- year: 2020
- doi_or_pmid: 不适用
- full_text_link: http://www.cnki.net
- is_open_access: 否

## 2. 化合物信息  

- compound_name: 聚乙烯热收缩膜 (Polyethylene Heat-shrinkable membranes)

- cas_number: 不适用

- molecular_weight: 不适用

- structure_image: 不适用

## 3. 实验设计  

3.1 动物模型  

- species: 小鼠 (Mus musculus)
- strain: 昆明种 , SPF级
- sex: 雌雄各半
- age: 不适用
- weight: 18-21g
- housing_conditions: 屏障系统饲养, 温度20-25℃, 相对湿度40%-70%
3.2 分组与给药  

- group_info: 采用限量法，设一个剂量组，雌雄各10只
- doses: 10000 mg/kg BW
- administration_route: 经口灌胃染毒
- dosing_frequency: 一次性给药
- treatment_duration: 不适用
- observation_period: 14 天
- license_or_permit: 实验动物合格证号: SCXK(川)2013-19 ；饲养动物房合格证号: SYXK(川)2016-043

## 4. 毒性结果  

- ld50: > 10000 mg/kg BW
- noael_loael: 不适用
- mortality:

- …:

- appetite_weight: 体重持续增长，生长发育正常
- fur_behavior: 被毛光滑柔顺
- body_weight_changes: 试验期小鼠体重持续增长. 具体数据如下表所示：

| 性别 | 剂量 (mg/kg BW) | 动物数/只 | 0d 体重/g | 7d 体重/g | 14d 体重/g | 死亡数 | LD (mg/kg BW) |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 雌 | 10 000 | 10 | $18.8\pm0.8$ | $30.7\pm1.6$ | $35.9\pm2.4$ | 0 | > 10 000 |
| 雄 | 10 000 | 10 | $20.0\pm1.2$ | $32.5\pm2.0$ | $41.5\pm2.1$ | 0 | > 10 000 |

- toxicity_classification: 实际无毒级 (nontoxic class)

## 5. 器官毒性与病理学

- gross_pathology: 未见明显的毒性反应
- liver: 外观颜色、形状大小、表面黏膜附着等情况都显示正常
- kidney: 外观颜色、形状大小、表面黏膜附着等情况都显示正常
- heart: 未提及
- spleen: 外观颜色、形状大小、表面黏膜附着等情况都显示正常
- lung: 未提及
- others: 胃形状、大小、内容物性状、胃黏膜均正常
- organ_weight_ratios: 未提及
- liver: 未提及
- kidney: 未提及
- heart: 未提及

- **潜在毒性机制（如有）**: PE本身及制备过程中的添加剂在与食品接触的过程中，会发生迁移效应，对食品安全性有一定影响 。
- **是否支持构建预测模型**: 是，可用于无毒/低毒食品包装材料建模。
- **研究局限性**: 未考察长期毒性。
- **你的备注或判断**: 数据完整、实验设计合理，结果可信，适合作为食品包装材料安全性评价参考样本。

## 4. 毒性结果

- **ld50**:
- **All-components**: LD₅₀ could not be determined; MTD was 16.0 g/kg·d.
- **Water extract**: LD₅₀ = 93.578 g/kg·d (95% CI: 89.149 - 98.484 g/kg·d).
- **Alcohol extract**: LD₅₀ = 61.388 g/kg·d (95% CI: 57.466 - 65.521 g/kg·d).
- **noael_loael**: Not specified in the article
- **mortality**:
- **Water Extract**:

| Dose (g/kg) | Number of Animals | Deaths | Mortality Rate (%) |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 115.0 | 20 | 18 | 90 |
| 102.4 | 20 | 13 | 65 |
| 91.1 | 20 | 10 | 50 |
| 81.1 | 20 | 5 | 25 |
| 72.2 | 20 | 0 | 0 |

- **Alcohol Extract**:

| Dose (g/kg) | Number of Animals | Deaths | Mortality Rate (%) |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| 85.75 | 20 | 20 | 100 |
| 73.00 | 20 | 14 | 70 |
| 62.00 | 20 | 10 | 50 |
| 52.75 | 20 | 6 | 30 |
| 44.75 | 20 | 1 | 5 |

- **clinical_signs**:
- **activity_changes**: The main toxic symptoms included convulsions, tetraplegia, and respiratory depression.
- **appetite_weight**: Not specified in the article.
- **fur_behavior**: Diarrhoea was observed as a main toxic symptom. Deaths primarily occurred within 48 hours for both water and alcohol extract groups.
- **body_weight_changes**: Mice in the treatment groups for both water and alcohol extracts showed a significant decrease in body weight during the first few days post-administration compared to the control group, followed by a gradual recovery in the surviving animals.
- **toxicity_classification**: Not specified in the article

## 5. 器官毒性与病理学

### 5.1 器官检查

- **gross_pathology**: Not specified in the article
- **organ_weight_ratios**: Not specified in the article
- **gross_observation**: Not specified in the article

### 5.2 组织病理（HE染色）

- **histopathology**: Not specified in the article
- **pathology_scoring**: Not specified in the article
- **histology_images**: Not specified in the article

## 6. 血液生化与生理指标

- **alt_ast**: Not specified in the article
- **akp**: Not specified in the article
- **tbil**: Not specified in the article
- **bun_cr**: Not specified in the article
- **hematology**: Not specified in the article
- **cytokines**: Not specified in the article
- **other_parameters**: Not specified in the article

## 7. 曲线拟合与效力参数

- **dose_response_model**: LD₅₀ was calculated using the Bliss method.
- **ec50_ac50**: Not applicable
- **emax**: Not applicable

## 8. 作者结论与备注

- **作者主要结论**: The acute toxicity of the different Cortex Periplocae components in mice follows the order: alcohol extract > water extract > all-components.
- **潜在毒性机制（如有）**: Not specified in the article. The toxic symptoms, including convulsions and respiratory depression, suggest a potential impact on the central nervous system.
- **是否支持构建预测模型**: Yes, the study provides quantitative LD₅₀ values with confidence intervals for two different extracts and an MTD for a third, which is valuable data for modeling the toxicity of herbal preparations based on their extraction method.
- **研究局限性**: The study lacks pathological (gross and histopathology) and biochemical analysis, which would provide a more complete picture of organ-specific toxicity. The specific chemical constituents responsible for the toxicity were not identified.
- **你的备注或判断**: The study provides a clear comparison of the acute toxicity of three different preparations of Cortex Periplocae using standard LD₅₀ and MTD methodologies. The finding that the alcohol extract is most toxic and the crude (all-components) preparation is least toxic is significant for clinical safety considerations. The data is robust for an acute lethality study, but the absence of pathology and bloodwork limits the understanding of the underlying toxic mechanisms.

# Comparative Study on Acute Toxicity of Different Components of Fructus Bruceae in Mice
## 1. 文献基础信息
- title: 鸦胆子不同组分对小鼠急性毒性的比较研究 (Comparative Study on Acute Toxicity of Different Components of Fructus Bruceae in Mice)
- authors: 孙蓉 (SUN Rong), 杨倩 (YANG Qian), 张作平 (ZHANG Zuo-ping), 吕立里 (LV Li-li)
- journal: 中医药导报 (Guide of China Journal of Traditional Chinese Medicine and Pharmacy)
- year: 2010
- doi_or_pmid: Not specified in the document.
- full_text_link: https://www.cnki.net
- is_open_access: Not specified in the document.
## 2. 化合物信息
- compound_name: 鸦胆子 (Fructus Bruceae) 全组分 (all-components), 水提组分 (water extract), and 醇提组分 (alcohol extract)
- synonyms: Not specified in the document.
- cas_number: Not applicable.
- molecular_formula: Not applicable.
- molecular_weight: Not applicable.
- smiles: Not applicable.
- inchi_key: Not applicable.
- source: The compound is an extract from the fruit of *Brucea javanica(L.) Merr.*
- purity: 95% alcohol was used for the alcohol extraction.
- category_usage: Traditional Chinese Medicine
- structure_image: Not applicable.
## 3. 实验设计
### 3.1 动物模型
- species: Mus musculus (Mice)
- strain: SPF grade
- sex: Not specified in the document.
- age: Not specified in the document.
- weight: 20 ± 2 g
- housing_conditions: Not specified in the document.
### 3.2 分组与给药
- group_info: For each of the three extracts (all-components, water, alcohol), there were 5 dosage groups and one control group. Each dosage group contained 20 mice.
- doses:
- **All-components group:** 4.5, 3.83, 3.25, 2.76, 2.35 g/kg
- **Water extract group:** 6.2, 5.08, 4.15, 3.41, 2.79 g/kg
- **Alcohol extract group:** 4.93, 3.94, 3.16, 2.52, 2.02 g/kg
- administration_route: Oral gavage (ig)
- dosing_frequency: Single dose
- treatment_duration: 1 day
- observation_period: 14 days
- license_or_permit: SCXK (鲁) 20090001
## 4. 毒性结果
- ld50:
- **All-components**: $LD_{50} = 3.14 g/kg$ (95% CI: 2.9384 - 3.3489 g/kg)
- **Water extract**: $LD_{50} = 4.023 g/kg$ (95% CI: 3.7256 - 4.3366 g/kg)
- **Alcohol extract**: $LD_{50} = 3.320 g/kg$ (or 3.3198 g/kg) (95% CI: 3.0252 - 3.6612 g/kg)
- noael_loael: Not specified in the document.
- mortality:

| :--- | :-: | :---: | :---: |

| :--- | :-: | :---: | :---: |

| :--- | :-: | :---: | :---: |

*Source table compiled from data on page 5*

- clinical_signs:
- activity_changes: Not specified beyond general toxic symptoms.
- appetite_weight: Weight loss was observed in the initial period after administration, followed by recovery.
- fur_behavior: Diarrhea and cyanosis were the main acute toxic symptoms.
- body_weight_changes: Mice in all treatment groups showed an initial decrease in body weight for 1-2 days, after which their weight began to increase. The control group showed a consistent increase in weight.

## 5. 器官毒性与病理学
### 5.1 器官检查
- gross_pathology: Not specified in the document.
- organ_weight_ratios: Not specified in the document.
- gross_observation: Not specified in the document.
### 5.2 组织病理（HE染色）
- histopathology: Not specified in the document.
- pathology_scoring: Not specified in the document.
- histology_images: Not specified in the document.

- alt_ast: Not specified in the document.
- akp: Not specified in the document.
- tbil: Not specified in the document.
- bun_cr: Not specified in the document.
- hematology: Not specified in the document.
- cytokines: Not specified in the document.
- other_parameters: Not specified in the document.
## 7. 曲线拟合与效力参数
- dose_response_model: Bliss method
- ec50_ac50: Not applicable.
- emax: Not applicable.
## 8. 作者结论与备注
- **作者主要结论**: The acute toxicity of different Fructus Bruceae components in mice, from strongest to weakest, is: all-components extract > alcohol extract > water extract.
- **潜在毒性机制（如有）**: The paper concludes that the specific toxic components and their mechanisms require further research.
- **是否支持构建预测模型**: Yes, the data is suitable for modeling the acute toxicity of traditional Chinese medicine extracts.
- **研究局限性**: The study is limited to acute toxicity ($LD_{50}$) and does not investigate sub-chronic or chronic toxicity, nor does it include data on organ pathology or blood biochemistry.
- **你的备注或判断**: The study provides clear, quantitative data on the acute oral toxicity of three different extracts of Fructus Bruceae in mice. The experimental design is straightforward and the methodology for calculating $LD_{50}$ is standard. The results are valuable for a comparative safety assessment of these extracts. However, the lack of pathological and biochemical data limits a deeper understanding of the toxic mechanisms.

# 麻杏苦甘汤的急性毒性实验研究

## 1. 文献基础信息
- title: 麻杏苦甘汤的急性毒性实验研究 (Acute Toxicity Study of Ma-Xing-Ku-Gan Decoction)

- purity: 未提供
- category_usage: 中药复方/宣肺散寒，止咳平喘，清肺润燥
- structure_image: 未提供 (中药复方无此信息)

## 3. 实验设计
### 3.1 动物模型
- species: 大鼠 (SD大鼠), 小鼠 (ICR小鼠)
- strain: SPF级SD大鼠, SPF级ICR小鼠
- sex: 雌雄各半
- age: 6-8周龄
- weight: 大鼠 $(200\pm20)$ g, 小鼠 $(20\pm2)$ g
- housing_conditions: 室温 $(25\pm2)℃$, 湿度 $(50\pm10)%，$ 动物屏障中心饲养 。

### 3.2 分组与给药
- group_info: SD大鼠40只和ICR小鼠40只，分别随机分为空白组(NC)和麻杏苦甘汤给药组(MXKGT)两组，每组20只，雌雄各半 。
- doses: 大鼠给药量128 g/kg，小鼠给药量256 g/kg 。
- administration_route: 经口灌胃 。
- dosing_frequency: 一日内灌胃2次 。
- treatment_duration: 1天（给药后观察14天） 。
- observation_period: 14天 。
- license_or_permit: 实验动物使用许可证: SYXK(宁)2020-0001 。伦理号: IACUC-2024-009/IACUC-2024-010 。

## 4. 毒性结果
- ld50: 无法测出半数致死剂量 $(LD_{50})$ 。
- noael_loael: 未提及。
- mortality:
- dose_128g/kg (大鼠): 死亡 0/20
- dose_256g/kg (小鼠): 死亡 0/20
- clinical_signs: 未见明显毒性反应 。
- activity_changes: 未见异常行为活动 。
- appetite_weight: 摄食、饮水无统计学差异 $(P>0.05)$ 。
- fur_behavior: 外观、腺体分泌等未见明显异常 。
- body_weight_changes: 各时期体质量无统计学差异 $(P>0.05)$ 。
- toxicity_classification: 按文中结果可判定为无毒 。

## 5. 器官毒性与病理学
### 5.1 器官检查
- gross_pathology:
- liver: 未见明显异常 。
- kidney: 未见明显异常 。
- heart: 未见明显异常 。
- spleen: 未见明显异常 。
- lung: 未见明显异常 。
- others: 甲状腺、生殖系统未见异常改变 。
- organ_weight_ratios: 脏器系数差异无统计学意义 $(P>0.05)$ 。
- gross_observation: 大体解剖未见动物外观、皮下、各脏器有明显异常 。

### 5.2 组织病理（HE染色）
- histopathology:
- liver: 肝小叶结构清晰，肝细胞索和肝血窦呈放射状排列，胞浆丰富 。
- kidney: 肾小体结构完整，肾小球大小、形态正常，肾间质未见炎性细胞浸润 。
- heart: 心间细胞互相平行排列，有分叉，彼此吻合成网，细胞核卵圆形，胞浆丰富 。
- spleen: 脾小体结构完整，边界清晰，形态大小正常 。
- lung: 肺组织中可见大量肺泡，肺泡上皮细胞形态、大小正常 。
- others: 甲状腺滤泡边界清晰，形态正常；生殖系统形态、结构、大小正常 。
- pathology_scoring: 未提供。

## 8. 作者结论与备注
- **作者主要结论**: 麻杏苦甘汤在最大给药量下未引起动物急性毒性反应 。未见动物死亡，未见明显毒性反应 。体质量、摄食、饮水无统计学差异 。血清生化指标大部分无统计学差异，个别差异仍在正常范围且改变值较小 。病理学检测未见异常改变 。该组方安全可靠，为临床用药提供了较可靠的依据 。
- **潜在毒性机制（如有）**: 未提及。
- **是否支持构建预测模型**: 是，可用于中药急性毒性建模。
- **研究局限性**: 未提及长期毒性等。
- **你的备注或判断**: 实验设计合理，采用最大耐受量方法，结果表明麻杏苦甘汤急性毒性较低。数据完整，包含血清生化指标和病理学检查，结果可信，适合作为中药安全性评价参考样本。

# 龙脑的小鼠急性毒性实验研究

## 1. 文献基础信息
- title: 龙脑的小鼠急性毒性实验研究 (Acute Toxicity Study of Borneol in Mice)
- authors: 刘佳, 高敏
- journal: 中国卫生工程学 (Chinese Journal of Public Health Engineering)
- year: 2010
- doi_or_pmid: 10. 19937/j.issn. 1671-4199. 2010. 05. 013
- full_text_link: 未提供
- is_open_access: 否

## 2. 化合物信息
- compound_name: 龙脑 (borneol)
- synonyms: 冰片
- cas_number: 未提供
- molecular_formula: 未提供
- molecular_weight: 未提供
- smiles: 未提供
- inchi_key: 未提供
- source: 贵州立爽药业提供
- purity: 含量50%
- category_usage: 香料、药理
- structure_image: 未提供

## 3. 实验设计
### 3.1 动物模型
- species: 小鼠 (Mus musculus)
- strain: 昆明种 (Kunming species), 清洁级
- sex: 雌雄各半
- age: 6-8周龄
- weight: (20 ± 2)g
- housing_conditions: 实验室环境
### 3.2 分组与给药
- group_info: 正式实验分6组，剂量组、溶剂组、阴性对照组 。每组10只，雌雄各半 。
- doses: 0.464, 1.000, 2.150, 4.640 g/kg BW 。
- administration_route: 经口灌胃 。
- dosing_frequency: 1次/24小时 (预实验) 。正式实验为单次灌胃 。
- treatment_duration: 1天 。
- observation_period: 14天 。
- license_or_permit: 实验动物生产许可证: SCXK(黔)2002-0001, 实验动物环境使用许可证: SYXK(黔)2008-0012 。

## 4. 毒性结果
- ld50: 雄性小鼠: 1.71 g/kg BW (95% CI 1.26~2.33 g/kg BW) ；雌性小鼠: 2.00 g/kg BW (95% CI 1.37~2.91 g/kg BW) 。
- noael_loael: 未提及。
- mortality:
- dose_4.640 g/kg: 死亡 10/10 (雌雄各半)
- dose_2.150 g/kg: 死亡 7/10 (雌性3只，雄性4只)
- dose_1.000 g/kg: 死亡 0/10
- dose_0.464 g/kg: 死亡 0/10
- clinical_signs:
- activity_changes: 运动增加、运动失调、静卧 。
- appetite_weight: 饮食正常 。
- fur_behavior: 皮毛光滑、大小便正常、无异常分泌物 。
- body_weight_changes: 存活的各剂量组小鼠每天的生长体重和溶剂对照组、阴性对照组比较，无明显改变 (P > 0.05) 。
- toxicity_classification: 未提及。
- **体重数据**:
**表1 龙脑小鼠急性毒性实验小鼠体重观察(x±sg)**

|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
| 0.464 | 雌 | 5 | $21.6\pm1.1$ | $22.4\pm1.1$ | $24.1\pm1.1$ | $24.7\pm1.7$ | $26.8\pm2.1$ | $27.6\pm2.2$ | $28.3\pm2.0$ | $30.5\pm2.0$ |

| 正常对照 | 雌 | 5 | $21.2\pm10.4$ | $23.4\pm1.2$ | $23.7\pm1.4$ | $25.2\pm1.3$ | $25.7\pm1.4$ | $26.2\pm1.2$ | $27.0\pm1.4$ | $30.8\pm0.8$ |
| | 雄 | 5 | $21.8\pm1.2$ | $24.1\pm0.5$ | $25.4\pm0.2$ | $26.6\pm0.5$ | $26.6\pm1.2$ | $27.2\pm1.5$ | $27.8\pm0.8$ | $33.0\pm1.4$ |

## 5. 器官毒性与病理学
### 5.1 器官检查
- gross_pathology:
- liver: 未见异常

- histopathology:
- liver: 未见异常
- kidney: 未见异常
- heart: 未见异常

## 6. 血液生化与生理指标
- alt_ast: 未提及
- akp: 未提及
- tbil: 未提及
- bun_cr: 未提及
- hematology: 未提及
- cytokines: 未提及
- other_parameters: 未提及

## 7. 曲线拟合与效力参数
- dose_response_model: 未提及
- ec50_ac50: 未提及
- emax: 未提及

## 8. 作者结论与备注
- **作者主要结论**: 根据龙脑的急性毒性实验反应的主要表现和死亡小鼠的大体解剖可以初步判断, 龙脑为神经毒作用 。雄性小鼠LD₅₀为1.71 g/kg BW，雌性为2.00 g/kg BW 。
- **潜在毒性机制（如有）**: 神经毒作用 。
- **是否支持构建预测模型**: 是。
- **研究局限性**: 未提及。
- **你的备注或判断**: 实验设计合理，采用霍恩氏 (Hom's) 法确定了小鼠口服龙脑的LD₅₀值 。研究结果表明龙脑对小鼠具有急性毒性，且主要表现为神经毒性症状 。根据GHS分类标准，雄性小鼠的LD₅₀值 (1710 mg/kg) 属于第四类 (有害)，雌性小鼠的LD₅₀值 (2000 mg/kg) 属于第五类 (低毒)，这表明龙脑具有一定的口服毒性。数据完整可信，适合作为毒性评估参考样本。

## 8. 作者结论与备注
- **作者主要结论**: 龙藤筋骨片小鼠急性毒性实验结果表明，临床用量的266.7倍给药后，小鼠未见明显中毒反应，也未见死亡，提示龙藤筋骨片安全性良好。
- **潜在毒性机制（如有）**: 无
- **是否支持构建预测模型**: 是，可用于中药急性毒性评估
- **研究局限性**: 仅进行了急性毒性实验，未考察长期毒性。未进行血液生化和组织病理学检查。
- **你的备注或判断**: 该研究只关注了急性毒性反应，实验设计相对简单，虽然结果显示安全性良好，但缺乏血液生化和组织病理学等更深入的毒性评价指标，因此结论的严谨性有所欠缺。
